	          {
	            label: "货 源",
	            value: "goods",
	            tips: "请输入需要采购的商品或关键词"
	          },
	          {
	            label: "供应商",
	            value: "factory",
	            tips: "请输入需要的供应商或主营产品名称"
	          }
	        ],
	        searchActive: '货 源',
	        searchKW: null,
	        banners: banners,
	        classifyImg: classifyImg
	      },
	      methods: {
	        handleCommand: function(e) {
	          for (var index in this.searchList) {
	            if (this.searchList[index].value == e) {
	              this.searchActive = this.searchList[index].label;
	            }
	          }
	        },
	        submitSearch: function() {
				if(this.searchActive === '货 源') {
					window.open('http://www.youboy.com/spro?kw=' + this.searchKW);
				} else {
					window.open('http://www.youboy.com/scom?kw=' + this.searchKW);
				}
	        },
	        initCategory: function() {
	          var $els = $("#classifyItem .classify-item");
	          $('body').on('mouseover', '#classifyItem .classify-item', function() {
	              $(".pop-classify,.pop-classify-img").show();
	              var index = $els.index($(this));
	              $(".pop-classify-img .indexClassifyImg").removeClass('active');
	              $('.pop-classify-img .indexClassifyImg:eq(' + index + ')').addClass('active')
	              $('.pop-classify-wrap>.pop-classify-main').hide()
	              $(".pop-classify-wrap>.pop-classify-main:eq(" + index + ")").show();
	          })
	          $(".classify-left").on('mouseleave', function () {
	            $(".pop-classify,.pop-classify-img").hide();
	          })
	        },
	        loginCommand: function(command) {
	        	switch (command) {
	        		case 'userPage': {
	        			//头部导航-个人中心链接
	        			window.open("http://member.youboy.com/sale/index.do")
	        			break;
	        		}
	        		case 'loginOut': {
	        			//头部导航-退出链接
	        			window.open("http://shop.youboy.com/exit.html")
	        			break;
	        		}
	        	}
	        },
	        initDhBox: function() {
				//网站导航显示层
		        $(".hx_topDh,.hx_dhBox").hover(function() {
		            $(".hx_topDh").addClass("hx_topDhHover");
		            $(".hx_dhBox").show();
		        }, function() {
		            $(".hx_topDh").removeClass("hx_topDhHover");
		            $(".hx_dhBox").hide();
		        });
	        },
	        initSwipper: function() {
	            var swiper = new Swiper('.swiper-container', {
	                slidesPerView: 9, //底部一栏 品牌展示个数
	                direction: 'horizontal',
	                navigation: {
	                  nextEl: '.swiper-button-next',
	                  prevEl: '.swiper-button-prev',
	                },
	                autoplay:true,
	                loop : true
	              });
	        }
	      },
	      mounted: function() {
	        this.initCategory() // 类目
	        this.initDhBox() //网站导航显示层
	        this.initSwipper()
	      }
	    })
  </script>
 </body>
</html>
